***языческий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:языческий.html>язы́ческий</a> (16077)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">языческъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jazyčeskŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jazýk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-eskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐθνικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ethnikós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of or for a nation, heathen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***язычник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:язычник.html>язы́чник</a> (22620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ꙗзꙑчьникъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jazyčĭnikŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ꙗзꙑкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jazykŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tongue; nation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Modeled on Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἔθνος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">éthnos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> : <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐθνικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ethnikós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heathen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:язычник.html>язы́чник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jazýčnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:язычник.html>язы́чника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:язычник.html>язы́чники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:язычник.html>язы́чников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">язы́чница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pagan</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">heathen</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">not adhering to an Abrahamic religion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">polytheist</span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яичница.html>яи́чница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jaíšnica, jaíčnica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яичница.html>яи́чницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яичница.html>яи́чницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яичница.html>яи́чниц</a></b>)

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>и́ч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ца</b>

Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-яич-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ниц</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***яйцо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>яйцо́</a> (2383)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ajьce</i>, diminutive of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*aje</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂ōwyóm</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>яйцо́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jajcó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>яйца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>я́йца</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>яи́ц</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>я́иц</a><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Colloquial.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>egg
<dl><dd><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>я́йца</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рицу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>у́чат</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jájca kúricu ne účat</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't teach your grandmother to suck eggs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>ovum</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> testicle, ball, nut, nad, gonad
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>де́ржит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>я́йца</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná déržit jevó za <b>jájca</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">she's got him by the balls</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>яй<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>цо́</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 5*d^  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> смехоэротическом <a href = vnd.unilang:фольклор.html>фолькло́ре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:используемый.html>испо́льзуемый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соблюдение.html>соблюде́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:музыкальный.html>музыка́льного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ритм.html>ри́тма</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:произношение.html>произноше́ния</a> им. п. мн. ч.: <i>я́ица</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ются</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> просторечные <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:произношение.html>произноше́ния</a> им. п. мн. ч.: <i>я́йцы, я́ицы</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-яйц-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-о</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jako</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> like, as</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> for, because</li></ol>

***якобы.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:якобы.html>я́кобы</a> (2422)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:якобы.html>я́кобы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jákoby</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>allegedly, supposedly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утверждать.html>утвержда́ет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:якобы.html>я́кобы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ет</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On utverždájet, što <b>jákoby</b> ničevó ne znájet.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He claims that he doesn't know anything.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***якорь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:якорь.html>я́корь</a> (9810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ѧкорь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ękorĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ancora</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">anchor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Swedish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Swedish">Old Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmq-osw">ankari</i> (gt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">ankare</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">akkeri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄγκυρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ánkura</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">anchor; hook</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:якорь.html>я́корь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jákorʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:якорь.html>я́коря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:якорь.html>якоря́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:якорь.html>якоре́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>anchor
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:якорь.html>я́корь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задница.html>за́дницу</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jákorʹ</b> mne v zádnicu!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">an <b>anchor</b> into my ass! (expression of utter bewilderment or disapproval)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(electrical)</i> armature core, armature</li>
<li><i>(acoustic)</i> reed</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:яловый.html>я́ловый</a> (23515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ꙗловыи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jalovyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jalovъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">barren, infertile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***яма.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́ма</a> (2213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́ма</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jama</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ama</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́ма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jáma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́мы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́м</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pit, hole (in the ground)</li>
<li>dungeon</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оркестровый.html>оркестро́вая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́ма</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">orkestróvaja jáma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">यम</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yama</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***ямочка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ямочка.html>я́мочка</a> (14140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямка.html>я́мка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jámka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямочка.html>я́мочка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jámočka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямочка.html>я́мочки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямочка.html>я́мочки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямочка.html>я́мочек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямка.html>я́мка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jámka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>, <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́ма</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jáma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (small) hole, pit, socket; dimple</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>моч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>

***ямщик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ямщик.html>ямщи́к</a> (27126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ямьщикъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jamĭščikŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">ямчы</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yamçı</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">yamçı</i>. Ending modified under the influence of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-щик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ščik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямщик.html>ямщи́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jamščík</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямщик.html>ямщика́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямщик.html>ямщики́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ямщик.html>ямщико́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>driver, coachman, charioteer, cabman, postilion engaged in transporting people and cargo by horse and carriage</li>
<li>Eurasian nuthatch <i>(Sitta europaea)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal jargon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fence; brothel keeper</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извозчик.html>изво́зчик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izvózčik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кучер.html>ку́чер</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kúčer</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возница.html>возни́ца</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vozníca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">генуарии</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">genuarii</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Γενάρης</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Genárēs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Ἰανουάριος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Ianouários</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">iānuārius</i>, from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Iānus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">god in Rome mythology</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from (perhaps) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ei-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:янки.html>я́нки</a> (21653)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Yankee</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:янки.html>я́нки</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jánki</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Yankee</li></ol>

<p><b>я́н<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ки</b>

***янтарь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:янтарь.html>янта́рь</a> (23865)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Phoenician_language" class="extiw" title="w:Phoenician language">Phoenician</a></span> <i class="Phnx mention" lang="phn">𐤉𐤍𐤕𐤓</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="phn-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yntr</span> <span class="ts mention-ts Latn">/yainitar/</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sea-resin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">gintaras</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">dzintars</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:янтарь.html>янта́рь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jantárʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:янтарь.html>янтаря́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:янтарь.html>янтари́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:янтарь.html>янтаре́й</a></b>)
</p>

***яранга.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:яранга.html>яра́нга</a> (32368)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chukchi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chukchi language">Chukchi</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ckt">яраӈы</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яранга.html>яра́нга</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jaránga</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яранга.html>яра́нги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яранга.html>яра́нги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яранга.html>яра́нг</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>yaranga <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a rounded or conical tent of reindeer hide, the traditional mobile home of some nomadic indigenous peoples of Russia.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:рана.html>ра́н</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:га.html>га</a></b>

***яркий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:яркий.html>я́ркий</a> (1246)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ꙗръкꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jarŭkyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jarъkъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jaro</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jarъ</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ъkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яркий.html>я́ркий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">járkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)я́рче</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярчайший.html>ярча́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bright</li></ol>

***ярлык.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлы́к</a> (16877)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">ярлыг</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yarlığ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлы́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jarlýk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлыка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлыки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлыко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> yarligh <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a written decree in the Mongol Empire and its <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Division_of_the_Mongol_Empire" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Division of the Mongol Empire">successor states</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1865</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9A%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%BF%D0%BE%D0%B2,_%D0%93%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%B0%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%A4%D1%91%D0%B4%D0%BE%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:ru:Карпов, Геннадий Фёдорович">Геннадій Карповъ (Gennady Karpov)</a>,  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очерк.html>о́черки</a> изъ исторіи россіиской <a href = vnd.unilang:церковный.html>церко́вной</a> іерархіи</span></cite>, Moscow:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Метрополитъ Петръ, такъ <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> какъ <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> другіе, ѣздилъ въ <a href = vnd.unilang:орда.html>Орду́</a>; подъ 1313 годомъ въ лѣтописи <a href = vnd.unilang:говориться.html>говори́тся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:князь.html>Князь</a> Великій Михаилъ Ярославичъ <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> съ нимъ Митрополитъ Петръ <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пошли́</a> въ <a href = vnd.unilang:орда.html>Орду́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> въ Ордѣ Ханъ Узвекъ сѣлъ, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> обнови́лось, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> всѣ <a href = vnd.unilang:приходить.html>приходи́ли</a> въ <a href = vnd.unilang:орда.html>Орду́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлыки́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>бра́ли</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мя</a>. митрополи́тъ Петръ былъ въ Ордѣ <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хан.html>Ха́на</a> въ <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>велико</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:честь.html>чести</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> отпущенъ былъ отъ <a href = vnd.unilang:хан.html>Ха́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> мно́гою честію <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:управа.html>упра́вою</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:русь.html>Русь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> всѣ <a href = vnd.unilang:православный.html>Правосла́вные</a> Христіяне встрѣчали <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> мно́гою <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́достью</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Metropolit Petr, tak že kak i drugije, jězdil v Ordu; pod 1313 godom v lětopisi govorítsja, što Knjazʹ Velikij Mixail Jaroslavič i s nim Mitropolit Petr pošlí v Ordu, po tomu što v Ordě Xan Uzvek sěl, i vse obnovílosʹ, i vsě prixodíli v Ordu i <b>jarlykí</b> bráli, káždyj na svojó ímja. Mitropolít Petr byl v Ordě u Xana v veliko česti, i otpuščen byl ot Xana so mnógoju čestiju i uprávoju na Rusʹ, i vsě Pravoslavnyje Xristijane vstrěčali jevó po étomu so mnógoju rádostʹju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Metropolitan Peter, like the others, rode to the Horde; under the year 1313 in the records it is said that the Grand Prince Mikhail Yaroslavich and with him Metropolitan Peter went into the Horde, for in the Horde came to sit the Khan <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C3%96z_Beg_Khan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Öz Beg Khan">Öz Beg</a>, and all was renewed, and all went into the Horde and took <b>jarlygs</b>, every one on his name. Metropolitan Peter was in high honour in the Horde by the Khan and he with his board were released from the Khan with high honours to Rus, and all Orthodox Christians therefore met him with much glee.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>label, tag

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ярмарка.html>я́рмарка</a> (7683)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">jarmark</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Jahrmarkt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fair</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмарка.html>я́рмарка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jármarka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмарка.html>я́рмарки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмарка.html>я́рмарки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмарка.html>я́рмарок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fair (market), funfair, county fair, state fair</li></ol>

***ярмо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ярмо.html>ярмо́</a> (30619)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ꙗрьмъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jarĭmŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*arьmo</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*arьmъ</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂er-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмо.html>ярмо́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jarmó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмо.html>ярма́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмо.html>я́рма</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмо.html>я́рм</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>yoke <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">wooden <a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иго.html>и́го</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ígo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
